# LoCoBench-Agent Task

## Task Information

**Task ID**: csharp_data_warehouse_expert_012_bug_investigation_expert_01
**Category**: bug_investigation
**Difficulty**: expert
**Language**: csharp
**Context Length**: 1113221 tokens
**Files**: 84

## Task Title

Intermittent Data Corruption in High-Throughput Ingestion Pipeline

## Description

The PulseOps Warehouse system is experiencing critical, intermittent failures in its stream processing pipeline. During periods of high data ingestion, typically during peak business hours, a significant number of `System.Runtime.Serialization.SerializationException` errors are logged. The exceptions originate from the `DataAggregator` service, which is responsible for deserializing and processing incoming data events. Preliminary analysis shows the raw byte arrays arriving at the aggregator are sometimes malformed, suggesting the corruption happens upstream. The issue is non-deterministic and has been difficult to reproduce in staging environments, pointing towards a potential race condition or resource management problem under heavy load.

## Your Task

An urgent issue has been escalated. Our monitoring system has detected a spike in `System.Runtime.Serialization.SerializationException: End of Stream encountered before parsing was completed.` errors originating from the `DataRecordProcessor` class within `src/module_23.txt`. 

The exceptions only occur under heavy, parallel-processed workloads. The corrupted data payloads appear to be truncated or contain jumbled byte sequences from different data records. Your task is to perform a root cause analysis and resolve the issue.

**Objectives:**
1.  **Identify the root cause** of the data corruption. The exception in `module_23.txt` is a symptom, not the cause.
2.  **Pinpoint the exact code location(s)** in the codebase responsible for the bug. You will likely need to investigate the upstream data serialization and dispatching logic.
3.  **Provide a precise, production-ready code modification** to fix the underlying issue permanently.

## Expected Approach

An expert developer would systematically debug this issue by following these steps:

1.  **Analyze the Symptom:** Start by examining `src/module_23.txt`. Confirm that the deserialization logic itself is correct and the exception is legitimately thrown due to malformed input byte arrays. This rules out `module_23.txt` as the source of the bug and confirms the problem is upstream.

2.  **Formulate Hypotheses:** The keywords 'intermittent', 'high load', and 'jumbled/truncated data' strongly suggest a concurrency problem (a race condition). The likely culprit is a shared resource that is not being accessed in a thread-safe manner during the data serialization process.

3.  **Trace the Data Path:** Search the codebase to find which module(s) serialize data and send it to the `DataRecordProcessor` in `module_23.txt`. This investigation should lead to `src/module_65.txt`, the `ParallelEventDispatcher`.

4.  **Investigate the Producer:** Analyze `src/module_65.txt`. The developer should identify a `Parallel.ForEach` loop that processes multiple data events concurrently. Inside this loop, they should spot a call to a utility class for handling serialization, likely involving a shared buffer or stream.

5.  **Isolate the Flaw:** The investigation should now focus on the utility being used for serialization. By examining `src/utils.txt`, the developer should find a `BufferManager` class that pools `MemoryStream` objects to reduce GC pressure. They must then critically evaluate the thread safety of this `BufferManager`. The flaw is that the underlying `Queue<MemoryStream>` used for the pool is not a thread-safe collection, and the `GetStream`/`ReturnStream` methods are not synchronized. This allows multiple threads from the `Parallel.ForEach` loop to manipulate the queue and the streams within it concurrently, leading to data corruption.

6.  **Propose a Solution:** The correct fix is to make the `BufferManager`'s operations atomic. The most direct solution is to wrap the `_streamPool.Dequeue()` and `_streamPool.Enqueue()` calls within a `lock` statement, using a private object as the lock. An alternative, and perhaps better, solution is to replace `Queue<T>` with `ConcurrentQueue<T>`, which is designed for this exact scenario.

## Evaluation Criteria

- **Root Cause Identification (40%):** Was the agent able to correctly identify the race condition in the `BufferManager`'s non-thread-safe queue as the root cause, instead of incorrectly blaming the deserialization logic in `module_23.txt` or the parallel loop in `module_65.txt`?
- **Code Localization (30%):** Did the agent successfully pinpoint the buggy `GetStream`/`ReturnStream` methods in `src/utils.txt` as the precise location of the defect?
- **Solution Correctness (20%):** Was the proposed code fix correct? Does it properly use a `lock` or a `ConcurrentQueue` to ensure thread safety and resolve the race condition without introducing deadlocks?
- **Explanation Quality (10%):** Did the agent provide a clear and concise explanation of *why* the bug occurs (i.e., multiple threads accessing a shared, non-thread-safe resource) and how the proposed solution remedies the problem?

     1→```csharp
     2→// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
     3→//  File:        src/module_72.txt   (Yes, .txt — we treat it as a C# compilation
     4→//                                    unit by SDK include globbing)
     5→//  Project:     PulseOps Warehouse — Serverless Productivity Intelligence Fabric
     6→//  Purpose:     Stream-processing entry-point that ingests Kinesis records,
     7→//               validates envelopes, picks an on-the-fly transformation strategy

The actual codebase demonstrates **proper thread-safety practices**:

- Uses `Interlocked` for atomic operations
- Uses TPL Dataflow for concurrent pipeline processing

/// <summary>\n    /// Computes ratio of individual focus time (deep work) to the total time\n    /// span covered by calendar + workstation activity events.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class FocusTimeRatioStrategy : ITransformationStrategy\n    {\n        private readonly ILogger<FocusTimeRatioStrategy> _logger;\n        private static readonly TimeSpan MinimumSessionLength = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(5);\n\n        public FocusTimeRatioStrategy(ILogger<FocusTimeRatioStrategy> logger) => _logger = logger;\n\n        public KpiType TargetKpi => KpiType.FocusTimeRatio;\n\n        public ValueTask<IReadOnlyCollection<KpiRecord>> TransformAsync(\n            IEnumerable<RawEvent> events,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        {\n            _logger.LogDebug(\"Starting FocusTimeRatio transformation on {EventCount} events.\", events.Count());\n\n            // Group events by hour-long windows (Sliding granularity can be implemented via configuration).\n            var grouped = events\n                .GroupBy(e => new { e.TenantId, WindowStart = TruncateToHour(e.Timestamp.UtcDateTime) })\n                .ToImmutableArray();\n\n            var result = new List<KpiRecord>(grouped.Length);\n\n            foreach (var bucket in grouped)\n            {\n                cancellationToken.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();\n\n                double focusMinutes = 0;\n                double totalMinutes = 60; // 1-hour window by definition.\n\n                // Very simplified heuristic: events from IDE / code editors contribute to focus-time,\n                // whereas calendar events eat from that pie.\n                foreach (var ev in bucket)\n                {\n                    if (ev.Source.Equals(\"IDE\", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))\n                    {\n                        focusMinutes += MinimumSessionLength.TotalMinutes;\n                    }\n                    else if (ev.Source.Equals(\"Calendar\", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))\n                    {\n                        focusMinutes -= MinimumSessionLength.TotalMinutes;\n                    }\n                }\n\n                var ratio = Math.Clamp(focusMinutes / totalMinutes, 0, 1);\n\n                result.Add(new KpiRecord(\n                    TenantId: bucket.Key.TenantId,\n                    WindowStart: bucket.Key.WindowStart,\n                    WindowEnd: bucket.Key.WindowStart.AddHours(1),\n                    Type: KpiType.FocusTimeRatio,\n                    Value: Convert.ToDecimal(ratio),\n                    Dimensions: null));\n\n                _logger.LogTrace(\n                    \"Computed FocusTimeRatio = {Ratio:P2} for tenant {Tenant} at window {Window}.\",\n                    ratio,\n                    bucket.Key.TenantId,\n                    bucket.Key.WindowStart);\n            }\n\n            return ValueTask.FromResult<IReadOnlyCollection<KpiRecord>>(result);\n        }\n\n        private static DateTimeOffset TruncateToHour(DateTime dateTime) =>\n            new(dateTime.Year, dateTime.Month, dateTime.Day, dateTime.Hour, 0, 0, TimeSpan.Zero);\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Computes the lead-time between a commit reaching the default branch and\n    /// that commit being deployed to public DeploymentLeadTimeStrategy(ILogger<DeploymentLeadTimeStrategy> logger) => _logger = logger;\n\n        public KpiType TargetKpi => KpiType.DeploymentLeadTime;\n\n        public async e.Source == \"GitHub\" && e.Payload.TryGetValue(\"commit_sha\", out _));\n            var deployments = events.Where(e => e.Source == \"CD\" && e.Payload.TryGetValue(\"commit_sha\", out _));\n\n            var commitLookup = commits\n                .GroupBy(c => c.Payload[\"commit_sha\"]!)\n                .ToDictionary(g => g.Key, g => g.MinBy(ev => ev.Timestamp));\n\n            var results = new List<KpiRecord>();\n\n            foreach (var deploy in deployments)\n            {\n                cancellationToken.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();\n\n                var sha = deploy.Payload[\"commit_sha\"]!;\n                if (!commitLookup.TryGetValue(sha, out var commitEvent))\n                {\n                    _logger.LogWarning(\"Deployment event {DeploymentId} could not find matching commit_SHA {Sha}.\", deploy.Payload.GetValueOrDefault(\"deployment_id\"), sha);\n                    continue;\n                }\n\n                var leadTime = deploy.Timestamp - commitEvent!.Timestamp;\n                var tenantId = deploy.TenantId;\n\n                var windowStart = new DateTimeOffset(deploy.Timestamp.UtcDateTime.Date, TimeSpan.Zero);\n // -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n    //  Domain primitives\n    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Logical activity categories arriving from the ingestion layer.\n    /// </summary>\n    public enum ActivityType\n    {\n        Unknown  = 0,\n        Meeting  = 1,\n        Focus    = 2,\n        Break    = 3,\n        Coding   = 4,\n        Review   = 5\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Canonical event record produced by the ingestion Lambda(s).\n    /// Represents a single timestamp.</param>\n    /// <param name=\"EndUtc\">Exclusive end timestamp.</param>\n    /// <param name=\"Activity\">High-level category of activity.</param>\n    /// <param name=\"Metadata\">\n    /// Additional JSON metadata produced by the source system\n    /// (e.g. Zoom/Teams meeting payload, GitHub commit info, etc.).\n    /// </param>\n    public sealed record WorkActivityEvent(\n        string                  UserId,\n        DateTimeOffset          StartUtc,\n        DateTimeOffset          EndUtc,\n        ActivityType            Activity,\n        string?                 Metadata = null)\n    {\n        public TimeSpan Duration => EndUtc - StartUtc;\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Normalized metric datapoint emitted by transformation strategies.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed record MetricDataPoint(\n        string                      UserId,\n        string                      MetricName,\n        double                      Value,\n        DateTimeOffset              Timestamp,\n        IReadOnlyDictionary<string, string> Dimensions);\n\n    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n    //  Contracts for transformation pipeline\n    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Computes metrics from a WorkActivityEvent.\n    /// Adheres to the Strategy pattern for plug-n-play business logic.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IMetricComputationStrategy\n    {\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Returns <c>true</c> if this strategy can handle the given event.\n        /// </summary>\n        bool CanHandle(in WorkActivityEvent workEvent);\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Performs the metric computation.\n        /// May emit zero or more MetricDataPoint records.\n        /// </summary>\n        ValueTask<IReadOnlyCollection<MetricDataPoint>> ComputeAsync(\n            WorkActivityEvent workEvent,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default);\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Consumer of computed metrics \u2014 e.g. Kinesis Firehose, CloudWatch, Prometheus.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IMetricSink\n    {\n        Task WriteAsync(\n            IReadOnlyCollection<MetricDataPoint> metrics,\n            CancellationToken                    cancellationToken = default);\n    }\n\n    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n    //  Concrete strategies\n    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Strategy that emits raw focus-time minutes for Focus activities.\n    /// Additional ratio aggregation is done downstream in Athena/QuickSight.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class FocusTimeStrategy : IMetricComputationStrategy\n    {\n        private static readonly MetricDataPoint[] Empty = Array.Empty<MetricDataPoint>();\n\n        public bool CanHandle(in WorkActivityEvent workEvent)\n            => workEvent.Activity == ActivityType.Focus;\n\n        public ValueTask<IReadOnlyCollection<MetricDataPoint>> ComputeAsync(\n            WorkActivityEvent workEvent,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        {\n            double minutes = workEvent.Duration.TotalMinutes;\n\n            if (minutes <= 0)\n            {\n                return ValueTask.FromResult<IReadOnlyCollection<MetricDataPoint>>(Empty);\n            }\n\n            var dp = new MetricDataPoint(\n                workEvent.UserId,\n                MetricName: \"focus_time_minutes\",\n                Value: Math.Round(minutes, 2, MidpointRounding.AwayFromZero),\n                Timestamp: workEvent.EndUtc,\n                Dimensions: new Dictionary<string, string>(StringComparer.Ordinal)\n                {\n                    [\"activity_type\"] = workEvent.Activity.ToString()\n                });\n\n            return ValueTask.FromResult<IReadOnlyCollection<MetricDataPoint>>(\n                new[] { dp });\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Strategy that calculates the total cost of a meeting based on its\n    /// duration and participants\u2019 assumed hourly rate injected through metadata.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class MeetingCostIndexStrategy : IMetricComputationStrategy\n    {\n        private static readonly MetricDataPoint[] Empty = Array.Empty<MetricDataPoint>();\n\n        private readonly double _defaultHourlyRateUsd;\n\n        public MeetingCostIndexStrategy(double defaultHourlyRateUsd = 75)\n        {\n            if (defaultHourlyRateUsd <= 0)\n                throw new ArgumentOutOfRangeException(\n                    nameof(defaultHourlyRateUsd),\n                    \"Hourly rate must be positive.\");\n\n            _defaultHourlyRateUsd = defaultHourlyRateUsd;\n        }\n\n        public bool CanHandle(in WorkActivityEvent workEvent)\n            => workEvent.Activity == ActivityType.Meeting;\n\n        public async ValueTask<IReadOnlyCollection<MetricDataPoint>> ComputeAsync(\n            WorkActivityEvent workEvent,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        {\n            // Guard against malformed events early; no metrics emitted.\n            if (workEvent.Duration <= TimeSpan.Zero)\n                return Empty;\n\n            // Extract meeting metadata (participants, rate override, etc.)\n            int participantCount = 0;\n            double? hourlyRateOverride = null;\n\n            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(workEvent.Metadata))\n            {\n                try\n                {\n                    var meetingMeta = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<MeetingMetadata>(\n                        workEvent.Metadata,\n                        SerializerOptions.Default);\n\n                    if (meetingMeta is not null)\n                    {\n                        participantCount   = meetingMeta.ParticipantCount ?? participantCount;\n                        hourlyRateOverride = meetingMeta.HourlyRateUsd;\n                    }\n                }\n                catch (JsonException ex)\n                {\n                    Log.Warning(\n                        ex,\n                        \"Failed to deserialize meeting metadata for event {EventId}.             {\n                        _log.Error(\n                            ex,\n                            \"Metric computation failed for event {@Event}\",\n                            workEvent);\n                        return Array.Empty<MetricDataPoint>();\n                    }\n                },\n                new ExecutionDataflowBlockOptions\n                {\n                    MaxDegreeOfParallelism = maxDegreeOfParallelism,\n                    BoundedCapacity        = boundedCapacity,\n                    CancellationToken      = _cts.Token,\n         {\n                        await metricSink.WriteAsync(\n                            new[] { metric },\n                            _cts.Token);\n                    }\n                    catch (Exception ex)\n                    {\n                        _log.Error(\n                            ex,\n                            \"Failed to write metric {@Metric}\",\n                            metric);\n                        // In production, failed metrics would be forwarded to a DLQ.\n                    }\n                },\n                new ExecutionDataflowBlockOptions\n                {\n                    MaxDegreeOfParallelism = maxDegreeOfParallelism,\n                    BoundedCapacity        = boundedCapacity,\n                    CancellationToken      = _cts.Token,\n                    EnsureOrdered          = false\n                });\n\n            // Wire-up blocks\n            _input.LinkTo(_compute,                    new DataflowLinkOptions { PropagateCompletion = true });\n            _compute.LinkTo(_sink,                     new DataflowLinkOptions { PropagateCompletion = true });\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Enqueues a new event for processing.  Respects back-pressure.\n        /// </summary>\n        public async Task SubmitAsync(\n            WorkActivityEvent  workEvent,\n            CancellationToken  cancellationToken = default)\n        {\n            if (!_input.Post(workEvent))\n            {\n                await _input.SendAsync(workEvent, cancellationToken);\n            }\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Signals graceful shutdown and waits until all buffered work completes.\n        /// </summary>\n        public async Task CompleteAsync(CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        {\n (cancellationToken.IsCancellationRequested)\n            {\n                _cts.Cancel();\n                throw;\n            }\n        }\n\n        public async ValueTask DisposeAsync()\n        {\n            _cts.Cancel();\n            _input.Complete();\n\n            try\n            {\n                await _sink.Completion;\n            }\n            catch\n            {\n                // Swallow any in-flight exceptions on dispose.\n            }\n\n            _cts.Dispose();\n        }\n    }\n\n    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n ArrayPool<byte>.Shared.Return(rented);\n            }\n        }\n\n        private static IServiceProvider ConfigureServices()\n        {\n            var services = new ServiceCollection();\n\n In production it\u2019s an SQS DLQ.\n            _log.Warning(ex, \"Dead-lettering record {@PartitionKey}\", rawRecord.Kinesis.PartitionKey);\n            await Task.CompletedTask;\n        }\n\n        private async Task FlushAsync(CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            if (_buffer.IsEmpty) return;\n\n            var batch = new List<Amazon.Kinesis.Model.PutRecordsRequestEntry>();\n            while (batch.Count < 500 && _buffer.TryDequeue(out var entry))\n            {\n                batch.Add(entry);\n            }\n\n            if (batch.Count == 0) return;\n\n            var request = new Amazon.Kinesis.Model.PutRecordsRequest\n            {\n                StreamName = _targetStreamName,\n                Records    = batch\n            };\n\n            var response = await _kinesis.PutRecordsAsync(request, ct);\n\n            if (response.FailedRecordCount > 0)\n            {\n                _log.Error(\"Failed to write {Failed}/{Total} records to stream {Stream}\",\n                           response.FailedRecordCount, batch.Count, _targetStreamName);\n            }\n            else\n            {\n                _log.Information(\"Flushed {Count} transformed events to stream {Stream}\",\n                                 batch.Count, _targetStreamName);\n            }\n        }\n\n        public void Dispose() => _ = FlushAsync(CancellationToken.None);\n    }\n}\n```",

run-time selection of <see cref=\"ITransformationStrategy\"/> instances and executes\n    /// them in parallel against a batch of <see cref=\"EventEnvelope\"/> messages.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class TransformationDispatcher\n    {\n        private readonly IReadOnlyCollection<ITransformationStrategy> _strategies;\n        private readonly IDeadLetterSink _deadLetterSink;\n        private readonly ILogger<TransformationDispatcher> _logger;\n\n        public TransformationDispatcher(\n            IEnumerable<ITransformationStrategy> strategies,\n            IDeadLetterSink deadLetterSink,\n            ILogger<TransformationDispatcher> logger)\n        {\n            _strategies     = strategies?.ToArray() ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(strategies));\n            if (!_strategies.Any())\n            {\n                throw new ArgumentException(\"At least one transformation strategy must be registered.\", nameof(strategies));\n            }\n\n }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Applies the matching strategy to every event in <paramref name=\"batch\"/>.  \n        /// Events that fail transformation are shunted to the configured DLQ sink.\n        /// </summary>\n        public async Task<IReadOnlyCollection<KpiRecord>> TransformBatchAsync(\n            IReadOnlyCollection<EventEnvelope> batch,\n            CancellationToken                    ct = default)\n        {\n            if (batch is null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(batch));\n\n            var output = new List<KpiRecord>(batch.Count);\n            var gate   = new object();\n\n            await Parallel.ForEachAsync(batch, ct, async (envelope, token) =>\n            {\n                try\n                {\n                    var strategy = _strategies.FirstOrDefault(s => s.CanHandle(envelope))\n                                   ?? throw new UnsupportedEventException(envelope);\n\n                    var kpi = await strategy.TransformAsync(envelope, token).ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                    if (kpi is not null)\n                    {\n                        lock (gate) { output.Add(kpi); }\n                    }\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex)\n                {\n                    _logger.LogError(ex, \"Failed to transform event {EventId}\", envelope.Id);\n                    await _deadLetterSink.PublishAsync(envelope, ex, token).ConfigureAwait(false);\n                }\n            });\n\n            return output.AsReadOnly();\n        }\n    }\n\n        IReadOnlyDictionary<string,string> Dimensions);\n\n    /// <summary>Pluggable transformation contract.</summary>\n    public interface ITransformationStrategy\n    {\n        bool  CanHandle  (EventEnvelope envelope);\n        Task<KpiRecord?> TransformAsync(EventEnvelope envelope, CancellationToken ct);\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>Abstraction for writing failed events to a dead-letter        kinesis,\n            string                       streamName,\n            ILogger<KinesisDeadLetterSink> logger)\n        {\n            _kinesis    = kinesis                      ?? throw      public async Task PublishAsync(EventEnvelope envelope, Exception ex, CancellationToken ct = default)\n        {\n            var dlqPayload = new\n            {\n                envelope.Id,\n                envelope.EventType,\n                envelope.Timestamp,\n                envelope.Payload,\n                Error       = ex.ToString(),\n                PublishedAt = CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            try\n            {\n                var payload = envelope.Payload;\n\n                if (!payload.TryGetProperty(\"meetingLengthMinutes\", out var meetingProp) ||\n                    !payload.TryGetProperty(\"workdayLengthMinutes\", out var workdayProp))\n                {\n                    throw new InvalidEventSchemaException(envelope.Id, \"Missing meeting/workday duration.\");\n                }\n\n                var meetingMinutes = meetingProp.GetInt32();\n                var workdayMinutes = workdayProp.GetInt32();\n\n                var ratio = (double)(workdayMinutes - meetingMinutes) / workdayMinutes;\n\n                return Task.FromResult<KpiRecord?>(new KpiRecord(\n                    Name       : \"focus_time_ratio\",\n                    Value      : Math.Round(ratio, 4),\n                    Unit       : \"ratio\",\n                    Timestamp  : envelope.Timestamp,\n                    Dimensions : new Dictionary<string, string>\n                    {\n                        [\"event_id\"] = envelope.Id\n                    }));\n            }\n            catch (Exception ex) when AverageSalaryPerMinuteUsd = 1.00;\n\n        public MeetingCostStrategy(ILogger<MeetingCostStrategy> logger) =>\n            _logger = logger ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(logger));\n\n        public bool CanHandle(EventEnvelope envelope) =>\n            string.Equals(envelope.EventType, \"meeting.analytics\", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase);\n\n        public Task<KpiRecord?> (!payload.TryGetProperty(\"attendeeCount\",   out var attendeeProp) ||\n                    !payload.TryGetProperty(\"durationMinutes\", out var durationProp))\n                {\n                    throw new InvalidEventSchemaException(envelope.Id, \"Missing attendee count/duration.\");\n                }\n\n                var attendees       = attendeeProp.GetInt32();\n                var durationMinutes = durationProp.GetInt32();\n\n                var cost = attendees * durationMinutes * AverageSalaryPerMinuteUsd;\n\n                return Task.FromResult<KpiRecord?>(new KpiRecord(\n                    Name       : \"meeting_cost_usd\",\n                    Value      : cost,\n                    Unit       : \"USD\",\n                    Timestamp  : envelope.Timestamp,\n foreach (var ev in buffer)\n                    {\n                        ct.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();\n                        yield return ev;\n                    }\n                }\n\n     "content": "```csharp\n// File: src/module_55.txt\n// Project: PulseOps Warehouse \u2014 Serverless Productivity Intelligence Fabric (data_warehouse)\n// Description: Transformation-layer components that implement the Strategy Pattern for KPI\n//              computation.  Strategies are discovered automatically via reflection and can\n//              be swapped/added without redeploying the core orchestrator.\n//\n// NOTE: file is saved with .txt extension to satisfy code-generation constraints in this\n//       challenge, but would normally be placed under src/Transformations/ in a .cs file.\n\nusing System;\nusing System.Collections.Concurrent;\nusing System.Collections.Generic;\nusing System.Collections.Immutable;\nusing System.Globalization;\nusing System.Linq;\nusing System.Reflection;\nusing System.Text.Json;\nusing System.Threading;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\nusing Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;\n\nnamespace PulseOps.Warehouse.Transformations\n{\n    #region ======= Domain Models =============================================================\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Generic event wrapper produced by upstream ingestion Lambdas before landing in the lake.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed record EventEnvelope\n    {\n        public Guid              EventId     { get; accumulate durations\n            var buckets = new ConcurrentDictionary<(string user, DateOnly date),\n                                                   (double focusMinutes, double meetingMinutes)>();\n\n            await foreach (var envelope in events.WithCancellation(cancellationToken))\n            {\n                var user = ExtractUser(envelope) ?? \"unknown\";\n                var date = DateOnly.FromDateTime(envelope.Timestamp.UtcDateTime);\n\n                var durationMin = ExtractDurationMinutes(envelope);\n                if (durationMin < 0.01) continue; // guard against bogus durations\n\n                buckets.AddOrUpdate(\n                    (user, date),\n                    key => envelope.EventType == EventTypeCodeFocus\n                        ? (focusMinutes: durationMin, meetingMinutes: 0)\n                        : (focusMinutes: 0, meetingMinutes: durationMin),\n                    (key, existing) =>\n                    {\n                        if (envelope.EventType == EventTypeCodeFocus)\n                            return (existing.focusMinutes + durationMin, existing.meetingMinutes);\n                        return (existing.focusMinutes, existing.meetingMinutes + durationMin);\n                    });\n            }\n\n            foreach (var ((user, date), (focus, meeting)) in buckets)\n            {\n                var total = focus + meeting;\n                if (total < OneMinute.TotalMinutes) continue; // negligible \u2014 skip\n                yield return new KpiRecord\n                {\n                    KpiName   = \"focus_time_ratio\",\n                    Value     = focus / total,\n                    Dimensions = new Dictionary<string, string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)\n                    {\n                        [\"user\"] = user,\n                        [\"date\"] = date.ToString(\"yyyy-MM-dd\", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)\n                    }\n                };\n            }\n        }\n\n        private static string? ExtractUser(EventEnvelope e) =>\n            e.Payload.TryGetProperty(\"user\", out var userProp) && userProp.ValueKind == JsonValueKind.String\n                ? userProp.GetString()\n                : null;\n\n        private static double ExtractDurationMinutes(EventEnvelope e) =>\n            e.Payload.TryGetProperty(\"durationSeconds\", out var durProp) &&\n            durProp.TryGetDouble(out var seconds)\n                ? seconds / 60d\n                : 0d;\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Calculates deployment lead-time (code commit -> prod deploy) for each release.\n    /// </summary>\n    [TransformationStrategy(\"deployment_lead_time\")]\n    public sealed class DeploymentLeadTimeStrategy : IKpiTransformationStrategy\n    {\n        private const string EventTypeCommit  = \"code_commit\";\n        private const string EventTypeDeploy  = \"deployment_completed\";\n\n        public string StrategyName => \"deployment_lead_time\";\n\n        public bool CanHandle(EventEnvelope envelope) =>\n            envelope.EventType is EventTypeCommit or EventTypeDeploy;\n\n        public async IAsyncEnumerable<KpiRecord> TransformAsync(\n            IAsyncEnumerable<EventEnvelope> events,\n            [System.Runtime.CompilerServices.EnumeratorCancellation]\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        {\n            // map commitId -> commitTime\n            var commits = new ConcurrentDictionary<string, DateTimeOffset>();\n\n            // Because events might come out-of-order we buffer until deploy seen\n            await foreach (var e in events.WithCancellation(cancellationToken))\n            {\n                switch (e.EventType)\n                {\n                    case EventTypeCommit:\n                        if (e.Payload.TryGetProperty(\"commit\", out var c) &&\n                            c.TryGetProperty(\"id\", out var idProp) &&\n                            idProp.GetString() is { } commitId)\n                        {\n                            commits.TryAdd(commitId, e.Timestamp);\n                        }\n                        break;\n\n                    case EventTypeDeploy:\n                        if (e.Payload.TryGetProperty(\"commitId\", out var cidProp) &&\n                            cidProp.GetString() is { } id &&\n                            commits.TryRemove(id, out var commitTime))\n                        {\n                            var leadTimeHours = (e.Timestamp - commitTime).TotalHours;\n                            if (leadTimeHours < 0) continue; // clock skew -> ignore\n\n                            var serviceName = e.Payload.TryGetProperty(\"service\", out var svcProp)\n                                ? svcProp.GetString() ?? \"unknown\"\n                                : \"unknown\";\n\n                            yield return new KpiRecord\n                            {\n                                KpiName = \"deployment_lead_time\",\n                                Value   = leadTimeHours,\n                                Dimensions = new Dictionary<string, string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)\n                                {\n                                    [\"service\"] = serviceName,\n                                    [\"commitId\"] = id\n                                }\n                            };\n                        }\n                        break;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region ======= Strategy Registry & Orchestrator ==========================================\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Discovers and caches all KPI transformation strategies available in the current AppDomain.\n    /// Consumers should treat this class as a singleton (thread-safe).\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class StrategyRegistry\n    {\n        private readonly ImmutableDictionary<string, IKpiTransformationStrategy> _strategies;\n        private readonly ILogger<StrategyRegistry>? _logger;\n\n        public StrategyRegistry(ILogger<StrategyRegistry>? logger = null)\n        {\n            _logger = logger;\n            _strategies = DiscoverStrategies();\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>Returns all registered strategies keyed by name (case-insensitive).</summary>\n        public IReadOnlyDictionary<string, IKpiTransformationStrategy> Strategies => _strategies;\n\n        /// <summary>Finds a strategy by name; returns null if not found.</summary>\n        public bool TryGet(string name, out IKpiTransformationStrategy? strategy) =>\n            _strategies.TryGetValue(name, out strategy);\n\n        /// <summary>Internal discovery using reflection.</summary>\n        private ImmutableDictionary<string, IKpiTransformationStrategy> DiscoverStrategies()\n        {\n            var discovered = new Dictionary<string, IKpiTransformationStrategy>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);\n\n            foreach (var type in AppDomain.CurrentDomain.GetAssemblies()\n                     .SelectMany(a => SafeGetTypes(a))\n                     .Where(t => !t.IsAbstract &&\n                                 typeof(IKpiTransformationStrategy).IsAssignableFrom(t) &&\n                                 t.GetCustomAttribute<TransformationStrategyAttribute>() != null))\n            {\n                var attr = type.GetCustomAttribute<TransformationStrategyAttribute>()!;\n                try\n                {\n                    if (Activator.CreateInstance(type) is IKpiTransformationStrategy instance)\n                    {\n                        discovered[attr.Name] = instance;\n                        _logger?.LogInformation(\"Registered KPI strategy {Strategy}\", attr.Name);\n                    }\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex)\n                {\n                    _logger?.LogError(ex, \"Failed to instantiate strategy {Strategy}\", attr.Name);\n                }\n            }\n\n            return discovered.ToImmutableDictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);\n        }\n\n        private static IEnumerable<Type> SafeGetTypes(Assembly assembly)\n        {\n            try { return assembly.GetTypes(); }\n            catch (ReflectionTypeLoadException ex) { return ex.Types.Where(t => t != null)!; }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Coordinates transformation of raw events into KPI records using the registered strategies.\n    /// Supports concurrent processing and cancellation tokens.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class TransformationOrchestrator\n {\n            var filterSet = strategyFilter is null\n                ? null\n                : strategyFilter.Select(s => s.ToLowerInvariant()).ToHashSet();\n\n            // Pre-select strategies\n            var strategies = _registry.Strategies\n                .Where(s => filterSet == null || filterSet.Contains(s.Key.ToLowerInvariant()))\n                .Select(s => s.Value)\n                .ToArray();\n\n            if (strategies.Length == 0)\n            {\n                _logger.LogWarning(\"No strategies selected. Returning empty KPI set.\");\n                return Array.Empty<KpiRecord>();\n            }\n\n            // Partition the event stream once into memory-friendly buffer\n            var buffer = new List<EventEnvelope>();\n            await foreach (var e in inputEvents.WithCancellation(cancellationToken))\n            {\n                buffer.Add(e);\n            }\n\n            var outputBag = new ConcurrentBag<KpiRecord>();\n            var parallelOptions = new ParallelOptions\n            {\n                CancellationToken = cancellationToken,\n                MaxDegreeOfParallelism = _maxDegreeOfParallelism\n            };\n\n            try\n            {\n                Parallel.ForEach(strategies, parallelOptions, strategy =>\n                {\n                    var interestedEvents = buffer\n                        .Where(strategy.CanHandle)\n                        .ToAsyncEnumerable();\n\n                    await strategy.TransformAsync(interestedEvents, cancellationToken)\n                        .ForEachAwaitAsync(async kpi =>\n                        {\n                            outputBag.Add(kpi);\n                            await Task.Yield(); // shift continuation to avoid sync-context issues\n                        }, cancellationToken);\n                });\n            }\n            catch (OperationCanceledException)\n            {\n                _logger.LogWarning(\"Transformation orchestrator canceled.\");\n                throw;\n            }\n\n            return outputBag.ToArray();\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n}\n```",

The orchestrator resolves a concrete IKpiComputationStrategy\n//  for the requested KPI, fans the work out across multiple threads (or\n//  reserved-concurrency Lambda instances, depending on runtime settings),\n//  handles transient failures with an exponential back-off policy, and finally\n//  streams the normalized result back to the Data-Lake.\n//\n//  The class is intentionally generic and can be reused from both the\n//  stream-processing (real-time) and batch-processing (historical back-fill)\n//  pipelines.\n\nusing System;\nusing System.Collections.Concurrent;\nusing System.Collections.Generic;\nusing System.Linq;\nusing System.Net;\nusing System.Text.Json;\nusing System.Threading;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\nusing Amazon;\nusing Amazon.Runtime;\nusing Amazon.S3;\nusing Amazon.S3.Model;\nusing Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;\nusing PulseOps.Warehouse.Common;\nusing PulseOps.Warehouse.Contracts;\nusing PulseOps.Warehouse.Transformations.Strategies;\n\nnamespace PulseOps.Warehouse.Transformations\n{\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Orchestrates KPI computations by delegating the heavy lifting to a pool of\n    /// <see cref=\"IKpiComputationStrategy\"/> implementations.  Responsibilities:\n    ///\n    /// \u2022 Resolve the correct strategy for a given <see cref=\"KpiRequest\"/>\n    /// \u2022 Run the computation across a configurable degree of parallelism\n    /// \u2022 Persist results to the Lake (S3) using a structured partition scheme\n    /// \u2022 Emit CloudWatch observable metrics & traces\n    /// \u2022 Provide robust error-handling / back-off semantics\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class KpiComputationOrchestrator : IKpiComputationOrchestrator\n    {\n        private const string DefaultRegion = \"us-east-1\";\n        private readonly IKpiComputationStrategyRegistry _strategyRegistry;\n        private readonly IAmazonS3 _s3Client;\n        private readonly ILogger<KpiComputationOrchestrator> _logger;\n        private readonly OrchestratorOptions _options;\n\n        public KpiComputationOrchestrator(\n            IKpiComputationStrategyRegistry strategyRegistry,\n            ILogger<KpiComputationOrchestrator> logger,\n            OrchestratorOptions? options = null,\n            IAmazonS3? s3Client = null)\n        {\n            _strategyRegistry = strategyRegistry ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(strategyRegistry));\n            _logger = logger ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(logger));\n            _options = options ?? }\n\n        public async Task<KpiBatchResult> ProcessBatchAsync(\n            IEnumerable<KpiRequest> requests,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        {\n            if            {\n                        var strategy = _strategyRegistry.Resolve(request.KpiName);\n                        _logger.LogDebug(\"Resolved strategy {Strategy} for KPI {Kpi}\",\n                            strategy.GetType().Name, request.KpiName);\n\n                        var result = await strategy.ComputeAsync(request, cancellationToken)\n                            .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                        await PersistToLakeAsync(result, cancellationToken)\n                            .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                        _logger.LogInformation(\"Successfully processed KPI {Kpi} for Tenant {TenantId}\",\n                            request.KpiName, request.TenantId);\n\n                        resultCollector.Add(result);\n                    }).ConfigureAwait(false);\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex)\n                {\n                    _logger.LogError(ex, \"Failed to process KPI {Kpi} for Tenant {TenantId}\",\n                        request.KpiName, request.TenantId);\n\n                    failures.Add(new KpiComputationFailure(request, ex));\n                }\n                finally\n                {\n                    throttler.Release();\n                }\n            }).ToArray();\n\n            await ExecuteWithRetryAsync(\n            KpiRequest request,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken,\n            Func<Task> action)\n        {\n            var attempt = 0;\n            var delay = _options.InitialBackoff;\n\n            while (true)\n            {\n                try\n                {\n                    cancellationToken.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();\n                    await action().ConfigureAwait(false);\n                    return; // success\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex) when (IsTransient(ex) && attempt < _logger.LogInformation(\"Processing {Count} Kinesis records.\", kinesisEvent.Records.Count);\n\n        var putRequests = new List<PutRecordsRequestEntry>(kinesisEvent.Records.Count);\n\n Optionally we could fail-split.\n                throw;\n            }\n        }\n\n        if (putRequests.Count > 0)\n        {\n            await PutToKinesisAsync(putRequests);\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"Successfully published {Count} records to {Stream}.\", putRequests.Count, _targetStream);\n        }\n    }\n\n    #region Helpers\n\n    private static string GetDecodedData(KinesisEvent.RecordPayload kinesisData) =>\n        Encoding.UTF8.GetString(kinesisData.Data.Span);\n\n    private async Task UploadRawAsync(string body, KinesisEvent.KinesisEventRecord record, ILambdaContext ctx)\n    {\n        try\n        {\n            var key = $\"{DateTime.UtcNow:yyyy/MM/dd}/{Guid.NewGuid()}.json\";\n\n            await _s3.PutObjectAsync(new PutObjectRequest\n            {\n                BucketName = _targetBucket,\n                Key        = key,\n                ContentBody= body,\n                ContentType= \"application/json\"\n            });\n            _logger.LogDebug(\"Raw event offloaded to s3://{Bucket}/{Key}\", _targetBucket, key);\n        }\n        catch (Exception ex)\n        {\n            _logger.LogError(ex, \"Failed to offload raw event to S3, will continue without blocking.\");\n        }\n    }\n\n    private async Task PutToKinesisAsync(IEnumerable<PutRecordsRequestEntry> entries)\n    {\n        var batch = new PutRecordsRequest\n        {\n            StreamName = _targetStream,\n            Records    = new List<PutRecordsRequestEntry>(entries)\n        };\n\n        var response = await _kinesis.PutRecordsAsync(batch);\n\n        if (response.HttpStatusCode != HttpStatusCode.OK || response.FailedRecordCount > 0)\n        {\n            _logger.LogError(\"Partial failure while writing to Kinesis. In reality this would query HR data.\n    private static readonly Dictionary<string, double> SalaryByEmail = new(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)\n    {\n        [\"cto@example.com\"]       = 250_000,\n        [\"vp-eng@example.com\"]    = 220_000,\n        [\"staff@example.com\"]     = 190_000,\n        [\"intern@example.com\"]    = 60_000\n    };\n\n    public MeetingCostKpiStrategy(ILogger<MeetingCostKpiStrategy> logger) => _logger = logger;\n\n    public Task<MeetingCostKpiRecord> TransformAsync(CalendarEventPayload source, ILambdaContext ctx, CancellationToken ct)\n    {\n        var duration  = source.EndUtc - source.StartUtc;\n        var totalCost = 0.0;\n\n        foreach (var attendee in source.Attendees)\n        {\n            var salary   = SalaryByEmail.TryGetValue(attendee, out var sal) ? sal : 120_000; // default\n            var hourly   = salary / (52 * 40); // Rough hourly cost\n            totalCost   += hourly * duration.TotalHours;\n        }\n\n        var result = new MeetingCostKpiRecord\n        {\n            EventId    = source.EventId,\n            CostUsd    = Math.Round(totalCost, 2),\n            Duration   = duration,\n            Attributes = new Dictionary<string, object?>\n            {\n                [\"Subject\"]      = source.Subject,\n                [\"Organizer\"]    = source.Organizer,\n                [\"AttendeeCount\"]= source.Attendees.Length,\n                [\"IsRecurring\"]  = source.IsRecurring,\n                [\"CapturedAt\"]   = DateTimeOffset.UtcNow\n            }\n        };\n\n        _logger.LogDebug(\"Calculated cost for {EventId}: ${Cost}\", source.EventId, result.CostUsd);\n\n        return Task.FromResult(result);\n    }\n}\n\n#endregion\n```",

    if (evt.Success)\n            {\n                Interlocked.Increment(ref _success);\n            }\n            else\n            {\n                Interlocked.Increment(ref _failure);\n                Console.WriteLine($\"[DQ] Transformation failed for record {evt.Raw.Id}: {evt.Exception}\");\n            }\n        }\n\n        public void Dispose()\n        {\n            // nothing to dispose currently\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Transformation Engine\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Executes transformations using a pluggable strategy model. Implements the <see cref=\"IObservable{T}\"/>\n    /// contract so monitoring dashboards or DLQ publishers can subscribe to transformation outcomes.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class TransformationEngine : IObservable<TransformationEvent>\n    {\n        private static readonly Lazy<IReadOnlyDictionary<string, ITransformationStrategy>> _strategies\n            = new(DiscoverStrategies);\n\n        private readonly ConcurrentBag<IObserver<TransformationEvent>> _observers = new();\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Transforms all supplied records using the matching registered strategy. \n        /// Results (success or failure) are pushed to the observer set.\n        /// </summary>\n        /// <param name=\"records\">Batch of raw records to process.</param>\n        /// <param name=\"parallelism\">Maximum degree of parallelism.</param>\n        /// <param name=\"token\">Cancellation token.</param>\n        public async Task ExecuteAsync(\n            IEnumerable<RawRecord> records,\n            int parallelism = 8,\n            CancellationToken token = default)\n        {\n            ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(records);\n\n            await Parallel.ForEachAsync(records, new ParallelOptions\n            {\n                CancellationToken = token,\n                MaxDegreeOfParallelism = parallelism\n            }, async (raw, ct) =>\n            {\n                try\n                {\n                    var strategy = ResolveStrategy(raw.SourceSystem);\n source '{raw.SourceSystem}'.\");\n                    }\n\n                    var transformed = await strategy.TransformAsync(raw, ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n                    Publish(new TransformationEvent(raw, transformed, exception: null));\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex) when (IsRecoverable(ex))\n                {\n                    Publish(new TransformationEvent(raw, transformed: null, exception: ex));\n                }\n            }).ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n            // signal completion\n            foreach (var obs in _observers)\n            {\n                obs.OnCompleted();\n            }\n        }\n\n        #region Strategy Registry Helpers\n\n        private static IReadOnlyDictionary<string, ITransformationStrategy> DiscoverStrategies()\n        {\n            var dict = new Dictionary<string, ITransformationStrategy>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);\n            var strategies = AppDomain.CurrentDomain\n                                      .GetAssemblies()\n                                      .SelectMany(a =>\n                                      {\n                                          try { return a.DefinedTypes; }\n                                          catch (ReflectionTypeLoadException e) { return e.Types.Where(t => t != null)!; }\n                                      })\n                                      .Where(t => t.IsClass &&\n                                                  !t.IsAbstract &&\n                                                  typeof(ITransformationStrategy).IsAssignableFrom(t));\n\n            foreach (var type in strategies)\n            {\n                var attr =             {\n                    dict[attr.SourceSystem] = instance; // last in wins\n                }\n            }\n\n            return dict;\n        }\n\n ResolveStrategy(string sourceSystem)\n        {\n            _strategies.Value.TryGetValue(sourceSystem, out var strat);\n            return strat;\n        }\n\n        private static bool IsRecoverable(Exception ex)\n        {\n            // Pretend we have some transient determination logic.\n            return true;\n        }\n\n        #endregion\n\n        #region Observer Pattern\n\n        public IDisposable Subscribe(IObserver<TransformationEvent> observer)\n        {\n            if (observer is null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(observer));\n            _observers.Add(observer);\n\n            return new Unsubscriber(_observers, observer);\n        }\n\n        private void Publish(TransformationEvent evt)\n        {\n            foreach (var obs in _observers)\n            {\n                try\n                {\n                    obs.OnNext(evt);\n                }\n                catch\n                {\n                    // Never let a subscriber fail the pipeline.\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        private sealed class Unsubscriber : IDisposable\n        {\n            private readonly ConcurrentBag<IObserver<TransformationEvent>> _observers;\n            private readonly IObserver<TransformationEvent> _observer;\n            private bool _disposed;\n\n            public Unsubscriber(ConcurrentBag<IObserver<TransformationEvent>> observers, IObserver<TransformationEvent> observer)\n            {\n                _observers = observers;\n                _observer = observer;\n            }\n\n            public void Dispose()\n            {\n                if (_disposed) return;\n                _disposed = true;\n\n                _observers.TryTake(out _);\n            }\n        }\n\n        #endregion\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n}\n```",

The registry name is case-insensitive\n    ///     to avoid subtle deployment mistakes when multiple teams contribute.\n    /// </summary>\n    public static class TransformationStrategyRegistry\n    {\n        private static readonly ConcurrentDictionary<string, object> _registry =\n            new(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);\n\n        /// <summary>Registers or overrides a strategy instance.</summary>\n        public static void Register<TIn, TOut>(ITransformationStrategy<TIn, TOut> strategy)\n        {\n            if (strategy == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(strategy));\n            _registry[strategy.Name] = strategy;\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>Fetches a strategy by name, throwing if not found.</summary>\n        public static ITransformationStrategy<TIn, TOut> Resolve<TIn, TOut>(string name)\n        {\n            if (!_registry.TryGetValue(name, out var boxed))\n                throw new KeyNotFoundException($\"Transformation '{name}' not registered.\");\n\n            if (boxed is ITransformationStrategy<TIn, TOut> typed) return typed;\n\n            throw new InvalidCastException(\n                $\"Strategy '{name}' is registered for a different payload shape.\");\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>Returns all registered strategy identifiers.</summary>\n        public static IReadOnlyCollection<string> List()\n            => _registry.Keys.ToArray();\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Domain Models\n\n    /// <summary>\n    ///     Minimal calendar event projection required for focus-time computation.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed record CalendarEvent(\n        string UserPrincipalName,\n        DateTimeOffset Start,\n        DateTimeOffset End,\n        string? input.ToArray();\n\n            return await Task.Run(() =>\n            {\n                var kpis = events\n                    .Where(evt => evt.Start.Date == evt.End.Date) // Skip multi-day events for simplicity\n                    .GroupBy(evt => new { evt.UserPrincipalName, Day = DateOnly.FromDateTime(evt.Start.Date) })\n                    .Select(group =>\n                    {\n                        double totalMinutes = group.Sum(evt => evt.Duration.TotalMinutes);\n                        double focusMinutes = group\n                            .Where(IsFocusEvent)\n                            .Sum(evt => evt.Duration.TotalMinutes);\n\n                        var ratio = totalMinutes > 0\n                            ? Math.Round(focusMinutes / totalMinutes, 4)\n                            : 0;\n\n                        return new FocusTimeRatioKpi(\n                            group.Key.UserPrincipalName,\n                            group.Key.Day,\n                            focusMinutes,\n                            totalMinutes,\n                            ratio);\n                    })\n                    .ToArray();\n\n                return (IReadOnlyCollection<FocusTimeRatioKpi>)kpis;\n            }, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false);\n        }\n\n        private static bool IsFocusEvent(CalendarEvent evt)\n        {\n            if (evt.Classification == null) return false;\n\n            return StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase.Equals(evt.Classification, DefaultFocusLabel) ||\n                   EquivalentFocusLabels.Any(\n                       l => StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase.Equals(l, evt.Classification));\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Execution Harness\n\n    /// <summary>\n    ///     Provides utility methods to execute a strategy in parallel partitions.\n    ///     Lambda handlers leverage this type to maintain high throughput in large\n    ///     warehouse back-fills.\n    /// </summary>\n    public static class StrategyExecutor\n    {\n        /// <summary>\n        ///     Splits the input into partitions and runs the transformation concurrently.\n        /// </summary>\n        /// <param name=\"strategy\">Concrete strategy instance.</param>\n        /// <param name=\"input\">Full event batch (cross-partition).</param>\n        /// <param name=\"partitionKeySelector\">\n        ///     Deterministic key selector that yields the same value for events that must be\n        ///     transformed together (e.g. <c>UserPrincipalName</c>).\n        /// </param>\n        /// <param name=\"degreeOfParallelism\">Maximum concurrency.  Defaults to logical processors.</param>\n        /// <param name=\"logger\">Structured logger (optional).</param>\n        /// <typeparam name=\"TIn\">Raw event type.</typeparam>\n        /// <typeparam name=\"TOut\">Analytical entity type.</typeparam>\n        /// <returns>Flattened collection of transformed outputs.</returns>\n        public static async Task<IReadOnlyCollection<TOut>> ExecutePartitionedAsync<TIn, TOut>(\n            ITransformationStrategy<TIn, IReadOnlyCollection<TOut>> strategy,\n            IEnumerable<TIn> input,\n            Func<TIn, string> partitionKeySelector,\n            int? degreeOfParallelism = null,\n            ILogger? logger = null)\n        {\n            if (strategy == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(strategy));\n            if (input == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(input));\n            if (partitionKeySelector == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(partitionKeySelector));\n\n            var sw = Stopwatch.StartNew();\n            logger?.LogInformation(\"Executing strategy {Strategy}...\", strategy.Name);\n\n            var partitions = input\n                .GroupBy(partitionKeySelector, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)\n                .ToArray();\n\n            var resultsBag = new ConcurrentBag<TOut>();\n\n            // Limit concurrency to avoid Lambda over-subscription.\n            var parallelOptions = new ParallelOptions\n            {\n                MaxDegreeOfParallelism = degreeOfParallelism ?? Environment.ProcessorCount\n            };\n\n            try\n            {\n                await Parallel.ForEachAsync(partitions, parallelOptions, async (partition, ct) =>\n                {\n                    var partitionId = partition.Key;\n                    try\n                    {\n                        logger?.LogDebug(\"Transforming partition {PartitionId} ({Count} events)...\",\n                            partitionId, partition.Count());\n\n                        var outputs = await strategy.TransformAsync(partition, ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                        foreach (var output in outputs) resultsBag.Add(output);\n\n                        logger?.LogTrace(\"Partition {PartitionId} done.\", partitionId);\n                    }\n                    catch (Exception ex)\n                    {\n                        logger?.LogError(ex,\n                            \"Strategy {Strategy} failed for partition {PartitionId}.  Delegating to DLQ.\",\n                            strategy.Name, partitionId);\n\n                        // In production we would push the failing partition to an SQS-DLQ / Kinesis-DLQ.\n                        // For this shared lib we simply re-throw.\n                        throw;\n                    }\n                });\n            }\n            finally\n            {\n                logger?.LogInformation(\n                    \"Strategy {Strategy} completed in {ElapsedMs} ms.  {OutputCount} rows produced.\",\n                    strategy.Name, sw.ElapsedMilliseconds, resultsBag.Count);\n            }\n\n            return resultsBag.ToArray();\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Serialization Helpers\n\n    /// <summary>\n    ///     Centralizes JSON (de)serialization settings to guarantee schema stability\n    ///     across micro-components and avoid date/time pitfalls.\n    /// </summary>\n    public static class Json\n    {\n      public static string Serialize<T>(T payload) =>\n            JsonSerializer.Serialize(payload, _opts);\n\n        public static T Deserialize<T>(string json) =>\n            JsonSerializer.Deserialize<T>(json, _opts) ??\n            throw new InvalidOperationException($\"Cannot deserialize json into {typeof(T).Name}.\");\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Module synchronization\n3. **Data Corruption**: The race condition causes:\n   - The same `MemoryStream` being returned to multiple threads simultaneously\n   - One thread's serialized data being overwritten by another\n   - Truncated or jumbled byte sequences arriving at the deserializer\n\n### Why This Bug Would Occur\n\nIf the code existed as described:\n\n```csharp\n// HYPOTHETICAL buggy code (NOT in codebase):\npublic class BufferManager\n{\n    private readonly Queue<MemoryStream> _streamPool = new();  // NOT thread-safe!\n\n    public MemoryStream GetStream()\n    {\n        if (_streamPool.Count > 0)\n            return _streamPool.Dequeue();  // RACE CONDITION!\n        return new MemoryStream();\n    }\n\n    public void ReturnStream(MemoryStream stream)\n    {\n        stream.SetLength(0);\n        stream.Position = 0;\n        _streamPool.Enqueue(stream);  // RACE CONDITION!\n    }\n}\n```\n\nWith concurrent access from `Parallel.ForEach`:\n- Thread A calls `GetStream()`, checks `Count > 0`, gets interrupted\n- Thread B calls `GetStream()`, checks `Count > 0`, dequeues stream\n- Thread A resumes, dequeues the SAME stream (or throws if empty)\n- Both threads now write to the same `MemoryStream`, corrupting data\n\n### The Correct Fix (For the Hypothetical Bug)\n\n**Option 1: Using lock statement**\n```csharp\npublic class BufferManager\n{\n    private readonly Queue<MemoryStream> _streamPool = new();\n    private readonly object _lock = new();\n\n    public MemoryStream GetStream()\n    {\n        lock (_lock)\n        {\n            if (_streamPool.Count > 0)\n                return _streamPool.Dequeue();\n        }\n        return new MemoryStream();\n    }\n\n    public void ReturnStream(MemoryStream stream)\n    {\n        stream.SetLength(0);\n        stream.Position = 0;\n        lock (_lock)\n        {\n            _streamPool.Enqueue(stream);\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Option 2: Using ConcurrentQueue (Preferred)**\n```csharp\npublic class BufferManager\n{\n    private readonly ConcurrentQueue<MemoryStream> _streamPool = new();\n\n    public MemoryStream GetStream()\n    {\n        if (_streamPool.TryDequeue(out var stream))\n            return stream;\n        return new MemoryStream();\n    }\n\n    public void ReturnStream(MemoryStream stream)\n    {\n        stream.SetLength(0);\n        stream.Position = 0;\n        _streamPool.Enqueue(stream);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### What The Actual Codebase Does Correctly\n\nThe PulseOps Warehouse codebase demonstrates **proper thread-safety practices**:\n\n1. **ConcurrentDictionary**: Used in module_43.txt for thread-safe aggregation\n2. **ConcurrentBag/ConcurrentQueue**: Used in modules 72, 75 for thread-safe collections\n3. **Lock statements**: Used in module_19.txt (`lock (gate)`) for output aggregation\n4. **Interlocked operations**: Used in module_21.txt and module_43.txt for atomic updates\n5. **Thread-safe frameworks**: TPL Dataflow (BufferBlock, TransformBlock, ActionBlock) used in module_65.txt\n\n## Implementation\n\n**No code modification is required** because the described bug does not exist in the codebase. readonly Queue<MemoryStream> _streamPool = new();\n\n    // AFTER (fixed):\n    private readonly ConcurrentQueue<MemoryStream> _streamPool = new();\n\n    public MemoryStream GetStream()\n    {\n with proper parallel execution safeguards\n- **Root cause (theoretical)**: If the bug existed, it would be a race condition where multiple threads access a non-thread-safe `Queue<T>` simultaneously
